Mazel says, "This exhibit was the culmination of dozens of anti-Israel and anti-Jewish events in Sweden."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-138"><a href="#cite_note-138">[138]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="January_19.2C_2004_.28Monday.29">January 19, 2004 (Monday)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/January_2004&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: January 19, 2004 (Monday)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>Cargo ship <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=MS_Rocknes&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="MS Rocknes (page does not exist)">MS <i>Rocknes</i></a> with a crew of 30 including the pilot capsizes near <a href="/wiki/Bergen" title="Bergen">Bergen</a>, Norway at 1630 local time (1530 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UTC" title="UTC">UTC</a>). Two people are reported dead and 24 still missing the morning after the accident. The ship was carrying a heavy load of rocks for use as shielding on top of a gas pipeline to <a href="/wiki/Emden" title="Emden">Emden</a>, Germany, from the Norwegian <a href="/wiki/Ormen_Lange_(gas_field)" title="Ormen Lange (gas field)">Ormen Lange</a> offshore gas field.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-139"><a href="#cite_note-139">[139]</a></sup></li>
<li>The English Court of Appeal calls for an end to the prosecution of parents whose babies may have died of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sudden_Infant_Death_Syndrome" title="Sudden Infant Death Syndrome">Sudden Infant Death Syndrome</a> (cot death) in cases where the only evidence is contended expert testimony.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-140"><a href="#cite_note-140">[140]</a></sup></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/European_Space_Agency" title="European Space Agency">European Space Agency</a> releases detailed colour images of the surface of <a href="/wiki/Mars" title="Mars">Mars</a>, taken by its orbiting <a href="/wiki/Mars_Express" title="Mars Express">Mars Express</a> probe.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-141"><a href="#cite_note-141">[141]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/NASA" title="NASA">NASA</a>'s <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mars_Exploration_Rover_Mission" title="Mars Exploration Rover Mission">Spirit rover</a> arrives at its initial destination, a rock named "<i><a href="/wiki/Adirondack_(Mars)" title="Adirondack (Mars)">Adirondack</a></i>", and prepares for analysis.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-142"><a href="#cite_note-142">[142]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-143"><a href="#cite_note-143">[143]</a></sup></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/U.S._presidential_election,_2004" title="U.S. presidential election, 2004">U.S. presidential election, 2004</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Iowa_caucuses" title="Iowa caucuses">Iowa caucuses</a> yield unexpectedly strong results for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_Democratic_Party" title="United States Democratic Party">Democratic</a> candidates <a href="/wiki/John_Kerry" title="John Kerry">John Kerry</a>, who earns 38% of the state's delegates and <a href="/wiki/John_Edwards" title="John Edwards">John Edwards</a>, who takes 32%. Former front-runner <a href="/wiki/Howard_Dean" title="Howard Dean">Howard Dean</a> slips to 18%, and <a href="/wiki/Dick_Gephardt" title="Dick Gephardt">Richard A. "Dick" Gephardt</a>'s fourth-place (11%) finish<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-144"><a href="#cite_note-144">[144]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-145"><a href="#cite_note-145">[145]</a></sup> prompts him to end his presidential bid.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-146"><a href="#cite_note-146">[146]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Yigal_Amir" title="Yigal Amir">Yigal Amir</a>, assassin of <a href="/wiki/Yitzhak_Rabin" title="Yitzhak Rabin">Yitzhak Rabin</a>, plans to marry.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-147"><a href="#cite_note-147">[147]</a></sup></li>
<li>"<a href="/wiki/Snow_White_and_The_Madness_of_Truth" title="Snow White and The Madness of Truth">Snow White and The Madness of Truth</a>" displayed at a <a href="/wiki/Stockholm" title="Stockholm">Stockholm</a> museum is again vandalized. A Russian-Jewish artist floats another image in the pool, that of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mijailo_Mijailovic" title="Mijailo Mijailovic">Mijailo Mijailovic</a>, the murderer of Swedish foreign minister <a href="/wiki/Anna_Lindh" title="Anna Lindh">Anna Lindh</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-148"><a href="#cite_note-148">[148]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mar%C3%ADa_Aznar" title="José María Aznar">José María Aznar</a>'s government in Spain is dissolved prior to March general elections. He has said he will not run for a third term of office.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-149"><a href="#cite_note-149">[149]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="January_20.2C_2004_.28Tuesday.29">January 20, 2004 (Tuesday)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/January_2004&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: January 20, 2004 (Tuesday)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Canadian_federal_election,_2004" title="Canadian federal election, 2004">2004 Canadian Federal Election</a>: <a href="/wiki/Belinda_Stronach" title="Belinda Stronach">Belinda Stronach</a> officially announces her run for leadership of the <a href="/wiki/Conservative_Party_of_Canada" title="Conservative Party of Canada">Conservative Party of Canada</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-150"><a href="#cite_note-150">[150]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Martha_Stewart" title="Martha Stewart">Martha Stewart</a> pleads not guilty to five criminal counts that include conspiracy, obstruction of justice and securities fraud stemming from a sale of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ImClone" title="ImClone">ImClone</a> stock in 2001. Conviction on any of the charges against her could put Ms. Stewart in federal prison. The five counts carry a total prison term of 30 years and a <span class="nowrap">$1.25 million</span> fine.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-151"><a href="#cite_note-151">[151]</a></sup></li>
<li>Colonel <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Rashid_Abu_Shbak&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Rashid Abu Shbak (page does not exist)">Rashid Abu Shbak</a> of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Palestinian_Authority" title="Palestinian Authority">Palestinian Authority</a>, said that information was still coming in and the investigating team had been upgraded, but he had no new leads on who was behind the bombing attack of an American diplomatic convoy on October 15, 2002. Three people died in the attack. U.S. officials have been stopped from going to <a href="/wiki/Gaza_Strip" title="Gaza Strip">Gaza</a> since the attack. No decision has been made yet on when they might be allowed to return. Col. Shbak blamed <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israel</a> for the lack of progress in the investigation.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-152"><a href="#cite_note-152">[152]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="January_21.2C_2004_.28Wednesday.29">January 21, 2004 (Wednesday)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/January_2004&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: January 21, 2004 (Wednesday)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/International_Olympic_Committee" title="International Olympic Committee">International Olympic Committee</a> urges <a href="/wiki/Athens" title="Athens">Athens</a> to continue working round-the-clock for the <a href="/wiki/2004_Summer_Olympics" title="2004 Summer Olympics">2004 Summer Olympics</a>. The deadline is for August 13.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-153"><a href="#cite_note-153">[153]</a></sup></li>
<li>Norwegian <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Haakon_Magnus,_Crown_Prince_of_Norway" title="Haakon Magnus, Crown Prince of Norway">Crown Prince Haakon Magnus</a>'s wife <a href="/wiki/Mette-Marit,_Crown_Princess_of_Norway" title="Mette-Marit, Crown Princess of Norway">Crown Princess Mette-Marit</a> gives birth to a daughter, at 0913 local time (0813 UTC), at Rikshospitalet University Hospital in <a href="/wiki/Oslo" title="Oslo">Oslo</a>. The newborn princess, named Ingrid Alexandra, weighs in at 3,686 <a href="/wiki/Gram" title="Gram">grams</a> and is 51 cm tall. She is second in succession to the Norwegian throne.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-154"><a href="#cite_note-154">[154]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-155"><a href="#cite_note-155">[155]</a></sup></li>
<li>The latest <a href="/wiki/World_Economic_Forum" title="World Economic Forum">World Economic Forum</a> event opens in <a href="/wiki/Davos" title="Davos">Davos</a>, Switzerland, with a keynote address by <a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iranian</a> President <a href="/wiki/Mohammad_Khatami" title="Mohammad Khatami">Mohammad Khatami</a>.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Royal_Canadian_Mounted_Police" title="Royal Canadian Mounted Police">Royal Canadian Mounted Police</a> raid the residence of <i><a href="/wiki/Ottawa_Citizen" title="Ottawa Citizen">Ottawa Citizen</a></i> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Reporter" title="Reporter">reporter</a> <a href="/wiki/Juliet_O%27Neill" title="Juliet O'Neill">Juliet O'Neill</a> for the purposes of searching for evidence of leaked information in the <a href="/wiki/Maher_Arar" title="Maher Arar">Maher Arar</a> <a href="/wiki/Deportation" title="Deportation">deportation</a> <a href="/wiki/Scandal" title="Scandal">scandal</a>. It was widely denounced by media groups and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Civil_libertarian" title="Civil libertarian">civil libertarians</a></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="January_22.2C_2004_.28Thursday.29">January 22, 2004 (Thursday)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/January_2004&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: January 22, 2004 (Thursday)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mars_Exploration_Rover_Mission" title="Mars Exploration Rover Mission">Mars Exploration Rover Mission</a>: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/MER-A" title="MER-A">MER-A <i>Spirit</i></a> rover stops transmitting meaningful data and has thought to have gone into <a href="/wiki/Safe_mode_(spacecraft)" title="Safe mode (spacecraft)">safe mode</a>. The cause of this is unknown but the rover is still able to send back a simple acknowledgement tone.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-156"><a href="#cite_note-156">[156]</a></sup></li>
<li>Staff members of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_Republican_Party" title="United States Republican Party">United States Republican Party</a> are accused of infiltrating <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_Democratic_Party" title="United States Democratic Party">Democratic Party</a> computers and making copies of confidential files stored on the compromised computers. The infiltrations reportedly began in early 2002.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-157"><a href="#cite_note-157">[157]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Maher_Arar" title="Maher Arar">Maher Arar</a> sues the United States government for having deported him to <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syria</a> and not Canada, his country of citizenship. He was reportedly tortured in Syria.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-158"><a href="#cite_note-158">[158]</a></sup></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Enron_Corporation" title="Enron Corporation">Enron Corporation</a>: <a href="/wiki/Richard_Causey" title="Richard Causey">Richard Causey</a>, former chief accounting officer was indicted in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Houston,_Texas" title="Houston, Texas">Houston, Texas</a>, on federal charges of securities fraud and conspiracy for his role in masking Enron's faltering fiscal health in late 2001. He has pled not guilty.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-159"><a href="#cite_note-159">[159]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Zimbabwe" title="Zimbabwe">Zimbabwe</a>'s only independent daily newspaper resumes publishing.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-160"><a href="#cite_note-160">[160]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="January_23.2C_2004_.28Friday.29">January 23, 2004 (Friday)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/January_2004&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: January 23, 2004 (Friday)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/David_Kay" title="David Kay">David Kay</a> steps down from <a href="/wiki/Iraq_Survey_Group" title="Iraq Survey Group">Iraq Survey Group</a>. <a href="/wiki/George_Tenet" title="George Tenet">George Tenet</a> names former UN weapons inspector <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Charles_Duelfer" title="Charles Duelfer">Charles Duelfer</a> to succeed Kay.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-161"><a href="#cite_note-161">[161]</a></sup></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/International_Monetary_Fund" title="International Monetary Fund">International Monetary Fund</a> has joined the <a href="/wiki/World_Bank" title="World Bank">World Bank</a> in forgiving <span class="nowrap">US$4 billion</span> of the $6.5bn debt owed by <a href="/wiki/Nicaragua" title="Nicaragua">Nicaragua</a>, sharply reducing the nation's overall debt payments.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-162"><a href="#cite_note-162">[162]</a></sup></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/European_Space_Agency" title="European Space Agency">European Space Agency</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Mars_Express" title="Mars Express">Mars Express</a> orbiter directly detects water ice in the southern polar region of the planet <a href="/wiki/Mars" title="Mars">Mars</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-163"><a href="#cite_note-163">[163]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-164"><a href="#cite_note-164">[164]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/NASA" title="NASA">NASA</a>'s <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/MER-A" title="MER-A">Spirit</a> rover communicated with Earth in a signal detected by NASA's <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Deep_Space_Network" title="Deep Space Network">Deep Space Network</a> antenna complex near <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Madrid,_Spain" title="Madrid, Spain">Madrid, Spain</a>, at 12:34 Universal Time (<span class="nowrap">4:34 am</span> PST) this morning. The transmissions came during a communication window about 90 minutes after Spirit woke up for the morning on Mars. The signal lasted for 10 minutes at a data rate of 10 bits per second. Mission controllers at NASA's Jet Propulsion Laboratory, Pasadena, California, plan to send commands to Spirit seeking additional data from the spacecraft during the subsequent few hours.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-165"><a href="#cite_note-165">[165]</a></sup> The flight team for NASA's Spirit received data from the rover in another communication session that began at 13:26 Universal Time (<span class="nowrap">5:26 am</span> PST) and lasted 20 minutes at a data rate of 120 bits per second.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-166"><a href="#cite_note-166">[166]</a></sup></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Thai</a> man suspected of having <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/H5N1" title="H5N1">bird flu</a> died, according to the Public Health Ministry.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-167"><a href="#cite_note-167">[167]</a></sup></li>
<li>At least 51 people, including a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Groom" title="Groom">bridegroom</a>, were killed on Friday when a fire ripped through a makeshift wedding hall in the southern Indian state of <a href="/wiki/Tamil_Nadu" title="Tamil Nadu">Tamil Nadu</a> during a marriage ceremony.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-168"><a href="#cite_note-168">[168]</a></sup></li>
<li>An explosion has killed two people at <a href="/wiki/Zhengzhou" title="Zhengzhou">Zhengzhou</a> railway station, one of the People's Republic of China's biggest transport hubs.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-169"><a href="#cite_note-169">[169]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="January_24.2C_2004_.28Saturday.29">January 24, 2004 (Saturday)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/January_2004&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: January 24, 2004 (Saturday)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mars_Exploration_Rover_Mission" title="Mars Exploration Rover Mission">Mars Exploration Rover Mission</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/NASA" title="NASA">NASA</a> isolates the <a href="/wiki/Flash_memory" title="Flash memory">flash memory</a> aboard <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/MER-A" title="MER-A">Spirit</a></i> as the most probable cause of communications problems; work continues on a method to operate the rover without it.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-170"><a href="#cite_note-170">[170]</a></sup></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/MER-B" title="MER-B">MER-B <i>Opportunity</i></a> successfully lands on Mars and continues communications through all stages.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="January_25.2C_2004_.28Sunday.29">January 25, 2004 (Sunday)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/January_2004&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: January 25, 2004 (Sunday)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Georgia_(country)" title="Georgia (country)">Georgia</a>'s new president, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mikhail_Saakashvili" title="Mikhail Saakashvili">Mikhail Saakashvili</a>, is sworn in.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-171"><a href="#cite_note-171">[171]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Chess" title="Chess">Chess</a> player <a href="/wiki/Viswanathan_Anand" title="Viswanathan Anand">Viswanathan Anand</a> wins in group A of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Corus_chess_tournament" title="Corus chess tournament">Corus chess tournament</a>. Thirteen-year-old Norwegian prodigy, <a href="/wiki/Magnus_Carlsen" title="Magnus Carlsen">Magnus Carlsen</a>, wins in group C.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-172"><a href="#cite_note-172">[172]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/David_Kay" title="David Kay">David Kay</a> says, in his opinion, <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraq</a> had no banned <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Weapons_of_mass_destruction" title="Weapons of mass destruction">WMD</a> stockpiles: "I don't think they existed", Kay said, "What everyone was talking about is stockpiles produced after the end of the last (1991) <a href="/wiki/Gulf_War" title="Gulf War">Gulf War</a>, and I don't think there was a large-scale production program in the '90s."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-173"><a href="#cite_note-173">[173]</a></sup> David Kay also says that part of <a href="/wiki/Saddam_Hussein" title="Saddam Hussein">Saddam Hussein</a>'s secret weapons programme may have been hidden in <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syria</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-174"><a href="#cite_note-174">[174]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-175"><a href="#cite_note-175">[175]</a></sup> Syria denies receiving Iraq arms.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-176"><a href="#cite_note-176">[176]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesia</a> announces that millions of birds have died from <a href="/wiki/Avian_influenza" title="Avian influenza">avian influenza</a> in the last few months.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-177"><a href="#cite_note-177">[177]</a></sup></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Golden_Globe_Awards" title="Golden Globe Awards">Golden Globe Awards</a>: Major winners include <i><a href="/wiki/The_Lord_of_the_Rings:_The_Return_of_the_King" title="The Lord of the Rings: The Return of the King">The Lord of the Rings: The Return of the King</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Lost_in_Translation_(film)" title="Lost in Translation (film)">Lost in Translation</a></i>, and <i><a href="/wiki/Angels_in_America_(miniseries)" title="Angels in America (miniseries)">Angels in America</a></i>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Hungary_national_football_team" title="Hungary national football team">Hungarian</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Footballer_(soccer)" title="Footballer (soccer)">footballer</a> <a href="/wiki/Mikl%C3%B3s_Feh%C3%A9r" title="Miklós Fehér">Miklós Fehér</a> dies in a match between <a href="/wiki/S.L._Benfica" title="S.L. Benfica">Benfica</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Vit%C3%B3ria_Guimar%C3%A3es" title="Vitória Guimarães">Vitória Guimarães</a> in Portugal. Benfica will subsequently retire his number 29 shirt.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="January_26.2C_2004_.28Monday.29">January 26, 2004 (Monday)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/January_2004&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: January 26, 2004 (Monday)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>President <a href="/wiki/Hamid_Karzai" title="Hamid Karzai">Hamid Karzai</a> signs into law the new constitution of <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-178"><a href="#cite_note-178">[178]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Avian_influenza" title="Avian influenza">Avian influenza</a> has now been detected in a total of nine countries, with Pakistan and <a href="/wiki/Laos" title="Laos">Laos</a> as the latest additions. Pakistan has detected less dangerous strains H7 and H9. A six-year-old <a href="/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Thai</a> boy became the seventh victim in Asia, with another ten suspected cases in the country. Around <span class="nowrap">19 million</span> chickens have been slaughtered as a result of fighting the spread of the flu. The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/World_Health_Organisation" title="World Health Organisation">World Health Organisation</a> expresses concern about a serious human outbreak. (WHO)<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-179"><a href="#cite_note-179">[179]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-180"><a href="#cite_note-180">[180]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-181"><a href="#cite_note-181">[181]</a></sup></li>
<li>In <i><a href="/wiki/Fellers_v._United_States" title="Fellers v. United States">Fellers v. United States</a></i>, the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_Supreme_Court" title="United States Supreme Court">United States Supreme Court</a> unanimously reaffirms the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Miranda_Warning" title="Miranda Warning">Miranda Warning</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-182"><a href="#cite_note-182">[182]</a></sup></li>
<li>A federal judge in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Los_Angeles,_California" title="Los Angeles, California">Los Angeles, California</a>, declares a portion of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/USA_Patriot_Act" title="USA Patriot Act">USA Patriot Act</a>, banning "expert advice and assistance" to suspected foreign <a href="/wiki/Terrorism" title="Terrorism">terrorist</a> groups, to be <a href="/wiki/Constitutionality" title="Constitutionality">unconstitutional</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-183"><a href="#cite_note-183">[183]</a></sup></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Connecticut_House_of_Representatives" title="Connecticut House of Representatives">House of Representatives</a> of <a href="/wiki/Connecticut" title="Connecticut">Connecticut</a> votes unanimously to investigate the dealings of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Governor_of_Connecticut" title="Governor of Connecticut">Governor</a> <a href="/wiki/John_G._Rowland" title="John G. Rowland">John G. Rowland</a>, a step which might lead to <a href="/wiki/Impeachment" title="Impeachment">impeachment</a> proceedings. Rowland is accused of using state contractors for his personal gain.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-184"><a href="#cite_note-184">[184]</a></sup></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Department_of_Energy" title="United States Department of Energy">US Energy Department</a>'s Inspector General releases a report stating that guards at the <a href="/wiki/Y-12_National_Security_Complex" title="Y-12 National Security Complex">Y-12</a> <a href="/wiki/Enriched_uranium" title="Enriched uranium">enriched uranium</a> storage facility in <a href="/wiki/Oak_Ridge,_Tennessee" title="Oak Ridge, Tennessee">Oak Ridge, Tennessee</a>, have been cheating on <a href="/wiki/Security" title="Security">security</a> drills, possibly for 20 years.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-185"><a href="#cite_note-185">[185]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-186"><a href="#cite_note-186">[186]</a></sup></li>
<li>Top <a href="/wiki/Hamas" title="Hamas">Hamas</a> official <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Abdel-Aziz_al-Rantissi" title="Abdel-Aziz al-Rantissi">Abdel-Aziz al-Rantissi</a> offered a 10-year <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Truce" title="Truce">truce</a> if <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israel</a> would withdraw from territory occupied since 1967 and acknowledge the creation of a Palestinian state. Israel dismissed the peace offer as "ridiculous".<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-187"><a href="#cite_note-187">[187]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="January_27.2C_2004_.28Tuesday.29">January 27, 2004 (Tuesday)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/January_2004&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: January 27, 2004 (Tuesday)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>The People's Republic of China announces an outbreak of the deadly H5N1 strain of <a href="/wiki/Avian_influenza" title="Avian influenza">avian influenza</a> in the autonomous region of <a href="/wiki/Guangxi" title="Guangxi">Guangxi</a>, becoming the 10th country in Asia to do so.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-188"><a href="#cite_note-188">[188]</a></sup> There are suspected cases in <a href="/wiki/Hunan" title="Hunan">Hunan</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hubei" title="Hubei">Hubei</a> provinces.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-189"><a href="#cite_note-189">[189]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-190"><a href="#cite_note-190">[190]</a></sup></li>
<li>British Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/Tony_Blair" title="Tony Blair">Tony Blair</a> narrowly defeats a rebellion in his own party over the <a href="/wiki/Higher_Education_Act_2004" title="Higher Education Act 2004">Higher Education Bill</a> – a highly controversial bill to reform <a href="/wiki/Higher_education" title="Higher education">higher education</a> funding, including the introduction of increased and variable <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tuition" title="Tuition">tuition</a> fees. It is approved in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/British_House_of_Commons" title="British House of Commons">House of Commons</a> by 316 votes to 311.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-191"><a href="#cite_note-191">[191]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-192"><a href="#cite_note-192">[192]</a></sup></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/U.S._presidential_election,_2004" title="U.S. presidential election, 2004">U.S. presidential election, 2004</a>: Senator <a href="/wiki/John_Kerry" title="John Kerry">John Kerry</a> wins the <a href="/wiki/New_Hampshire_primary" title="New Hampshire primary">New Hampshire primary</a>. <a href="/wiki/Howard_Dean" title="Howard Dean">Howard Dean</a> comes second.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Academy_Awards" title="Academy Awards">Academy Awards</a>: nominations announced, leading films are <i><a href="/wiki/The_Lord_of_the_Rings:_The_Return_of_the_King" title="The Lord of the Rings: The Return of the King">The Lord of the Rings: The Return of the King</a></i> (11), <i><a href="/wiki/Master_and_Commander:_The_Far_Side_of_the_World" title="Master and Commander: The Far Side of the World">Master and Commander</a></i> (10), <i><a href="/wiki/Seabiscuit_(film)" title="Seabiscuit (film)">Seabiscuit</a></i> (7), <i><a href="/wiki/Mystic_River_(film)" title="Mystic River (film)">Mystic River</a></i> (6), and <i><a href="/wiki/Cold_Mountain_(film)" title="Cold Mountain (film)">Cold Mountain</a></i> (6). <a href="/wiki/Keisha_Castle-Hughes" title="Keisha Castle-Hughes">Keisha Castle-Hughes</a>, at 13, becomes the youngest nominee ever for the <a href="/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Actress" title="Academy Award for Best Actress">Academy Award for Best Actress</a></li>
<li>A new <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/E-mail" title="E-mail">e-mail</a> <a href="/wiki/Computer_worm" title="Computer worm">worm</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Novarg/Mydoom" title="Novarg/Mydoom">Novarg/Mydoom</a>, is spreading rapidly to thousands of machines running <a href="/wiki/Microsoft_Windows" title="Microsoft Windows">Microsoft Windows</a>. It rapidly becomes the fastest-spreading e-mail worm to date.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-193"><a href="#cite_note-193">[193]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-194"><a href="#cite_note-194">[194]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-195"><a href="#cite_note-195">[195]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-196"><a href="#cite_note-196">[196]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-197"><a href="#cite_note-197">[197]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-198"><a href="#cite_note-198">[198]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="January_28.2C_2004_.28Wednesday.29">January 28, 2004 (Wednesday)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/January_2004&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: January 28, 2004 (Wednesday)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Milan_Babic" title="Milan Babic">Milan Babic</a>, the former leader of the breakaway <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Serbian_Krajina" title="Republic of Serbian Krajina">Republic of Serbian Krajina</a> (now re-incorporated into <a href="/wiki/Croatia" title="Croatia">Croatia</a>), pleads guilty to <a href="/wiki/Crimes_against_humanity" title="Crimes against humanity">crimes against humanity</a> at the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ICTY" title="ICTY">International Criminal Tribunal for the Former Yugoslavia</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/David_Kay" title="David Kay">David Kay</a> testifies before a <a href="/wiki/United_States_Senate" title="United States Senate">United States Senate</a> <a href="/wiki/Committee" title="Committee">committee</a> stating that evidence of weapons of mass destruction was based on inaccurate <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Intelligence_(information_gathering)" title="Intelligence (information gathering)">intelligence</a>. "I believe that the effort that has been directed to this point has been sufficiently intense that it is highly unlikely that there were large stockpiles of deployed, militarized chemical weapons there" and, even if <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraq</a> did not have weapons stockpiles, this does not mean that nation was not dangerous. Kay urges for an <a href="/wiki/Inquiry" title="Inquiry">inquiry</a> into the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Intelligence_failure" title="Intelligence failure">intelligence failure</a> and states that the United States needed better intelligence.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-199"><a href="#cite_note-199">[199]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-200"><a href="#cite_note-200">[200]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-201"><a href="#cite_note-201">[201]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-202"><a href="#cite_note-202">[202]</a></sup></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Hutton_Inquiry" title="Hutton Inquiry">Hutton Inquiry</a> report is released, stating the <a href="/wiki/Suicide" title="Suicide">suicide</a> of <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraqi</a> weapons expert <a href="/wiki/David_Kelly_(weapons_expert)" title="David Kelly (weapons expert)">David Kelly</a> did not involve "dishonourable conduct" on the part of the United Kingdom's government and exonerates <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Prime_Minister" title="Prime Minister">Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Tony_Blair" title="Tony Blair">Tony Blair</a> of any wrongdoing in Kelly's death. The <a href="/wiki/BBC" title="BBC">BBC</a> receives harsh criticism for the allegations within <a href="/wiki/Andrew_Gilligan" title="Andrew Gilligan">Andrew Gilligan</a>'s report on <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Weapons_of_mass_destruction" title="Weapons of mass destruction">weapons of mass destruction</a> and the BBC's subsequent backing of the report. <a href="/wiki/Gavyn_Davies" title="Gavyn Davies">Gavyn Davies</a> takes full responsibility for any wrongdoing and resigns as the Chairman of the Board of Governors of the BBC.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-203"><a href="#cite_note-203">[203]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-204"><a href="#cite_note-204">[204]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-205"><a href="#cite_note-205">[205]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-206"><a href="#cite_note-206">[206]</a></sup></li>
<li>The discovery of a new form of matter, <a href="/wiki/Fermionic_condensate" title="Fermionic condensate">Fermionic condensate</a>, has been announced.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-207"><a href="#cite_note-207">[207]</a></sup></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/World_Wide_Web_Consortium" title="World Wide Web Consortium">World Wide Web Consortium</a> releases <a href="/wiki/Document_Object_Model" title="Document Object Model">Document Object Model</a> Level 3 Validation as a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/W3C_Recommendation" title="W3C Recommendation">W3C Recommendation</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-208"><a href="#cite_note-208">[208]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/San_Jose,_California" title="San Jose, California">San Jose, California</a>, mayor <a href="/wiki/Ron_Gonzales" title="Ron Gonzales">Ron Gonzales</a> suffers a mild <a href="/wiki/Stroke" title="Stroke">stroke</a> while giving the State of the City address. The mayor is expected to make a full recovery.</li>
<li>A rare artefact from the 1800s used against <a href="/wiki/Witchcraft" title="Witchcraft">witchcraft</a> is found in the United Kingdom. Now displayed in a museum.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-209"><a href="#cite_note-209">[209]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="January_29.2C_2004_.28Thursday.29">January 29, 2004 (Thursday)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/January_2004&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: January 29, 2004 (Thursday)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>A 60-ton <a href="/wiki/Sperm_whale" title="Sperm whale">sperm whale</a> carcass explodes in downtown <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tainan_City" title="Tainan City">Tainan</a>, <a href="/wiki/Taiwan" title="Taiwan">Taiwan</a>, causing traffic delays and showering vehicles and pedestrians with blood and entrails.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-210"><a href="#cite_note-210">[210]</a></sup></li>
<li>A report submitted today to the State of <a href="/wiki/Maryland" title="Maryland">Maryland</a> states that the <a href="/wiki/Electronic_voting" title="Electronic voting">electronic voting</a> <a href="/wiki/Voting_machine" title="Voting machine">machines</a> made by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Diebold_Election_Systems" title="Diebold Election Systems">Diebold Election Systems</a> "have such poor computer security and physical security that an election could be disrupted or even stolen by corrupt insiders or determined outsiders". The machines have been purchased by a number of states in the United States.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-211"><a href="#cite_note-211">[211]</a></sup> This is the third report to state that the machines do not meet the security requirements of an election. Previous reports are available online:,.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-212"><a href="#cite_note-212">[212]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-213"><a href="#cite_note-213">[213]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Hutton_Inquiry" title="Hutton Inquiry">Hutton Inquiry</a>: The <a href="/wiki/BBC" title="BBC">BBC</a> Director-General, <a href="/wiki/Greg_Dyke" title="Greg Dyke">Greg Dyke</a>, resigns in the continuing fall-out from the report. Mr Dyke is the second high-ranking BBC official to resign. <a href="/wiki/Mark_Byford" title="Mark Byford">Mark Byford</a> is appointed Acting Director-General.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-214"><a href="#cite_note-214">[214]</a></sup> The UK media in general condemns the report as a whitewash.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-215"><a href="#cite_note-215">[215]</a></sup></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Al-Aqsa_Martyrs%27_Brigades" title="Al-Aqsa Martyrs' Brigades">Al-Aqsa Martyrs' Brigades</a> of <a href="/wiki/Fatah" title="Fatah">Fatah</a> claim responsibility for a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Suicide_bombing" title="Suicide bombing">suicide bombing</a> aboard a city bus, in which <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Ali_Yusuf_Jaara&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Ali Yusuf Jaara (page does not exist)">Ali Yusuf Jaara</a>, a member of the <a href="/wiki/Palestinian_National_Authority" title="Palestinian National Authority">Palestinian</a> police force, kills 10 <a href="/wiki/Israelis" title="Israelis">Israelis</a> and wounds more than 50, outside the Prime Minister's residence in <a href="/wiki/Jerusalem" title="Jerusalem">Jerusalem</a>. Simultaneously with the bombing, <a href="/wiki/Shaul_Mofaz" title="Shaul Mofaz">Shaul Mofaz</a>, Israeli Defense Minister, is meeting with American envoys Wolfe and Sauterfield, who have requested an easing-up of conditions for the Palestinians. The explosion also coincides with a German-brokered prisoner swap between Israel and the Lebanese <a href="/wiki/Guerrilla_warfare" title="Guerrilla warfare">guerrilla</a> group <a href="/wiki/Hezbollah" title="Hezbollah">Hezbollah</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-216"><a href="#cite_note-216">[216]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-217"><a href="#cite_note-217">[217]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-218"><a href="#cite_note-218">[218]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="January_30.2C_2004_.28Friday.29">January 30, 2004 (Friday)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/January_2004&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: January 30, 2004 (Friday)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Hutton_Inquiry" title="Hutton Inquiry">Hutton Inquiry</a>: Reporter <a href="/wiki/Andrew_Gilligan" title="Andrew Gilligan">Andrew Gilligan</a> resigns from the <a href="/wiki/BBC" title="BBC">BBC</a> in the continuing fallout of the publication of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/James_Brian_Edward_Hutton" title="James Brian Edward Hutton">Lord Hutton's</a> report into the circumstances of the death of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Dr_David_Kelly" title="Dr David Kelly">Dr David Kelly</a>. This follows the earlier resignation of the <a href="/wiki/Director-General_of_the_BBC" title="Director-General of the BBC">Director-General</a> <a href="/wiki/Greg_Dyke" title="Greg Dyke">Greg Dyke</a> and chairman of the Board of Governors <a href="/wiki/Gavyn_Davies" title="Gavyn Davies">Gavyn Davies</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-219"><a href="#cite_note-219">[219]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-220"><a href="#cite_note-220">[220]</a></sup></li>
<li>Former French Prime Minister and current Mayor of <a href="/wiki/Bordeaux" title="Bordeaux">Bordeaux</a> <a href="/wiki/Alain_Jupp%C3%A9" title="Alain Juppé">Alain Juppé</a> is convicted of a party funding scam in the 1980s and early 1990s, and is given an 18-month suspended jail sentence and disqualified from elected office for 10 years, although he retains his <a href="/wiki/Mayor" title="Mayor">mayoralty</a> pending his appeal. He had been viewed as <a href="/wiki/Jacques_Chirac" title="Jacques Chirac">Jacques Chirac</a>'s likely successor in the <a href="/wiki/French_presidential_election,_2007" title="French presidential election, 2007">2007 Presidential election</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-221"><a href="#cite_note-221">[221]</a></sup></li>
<li>Muslims begin the annual <a href="/wiki/Hajj" title="Hajj">Hajj</a> today amid fears of a possible attack by Saudi-born <a href="/wiki/Osama_bin_Laden" title="Osama bin Laden">Osama bin Laden</a>'s <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Al_Qaeda" title="Al Qaeda">al Qaeda</a> network.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-222"><a href="#cite_note-222">[222]</a></sup></li>
<li>Sheik <a href="/wiki/Ahmed_Yassin" title="Ahmed Yassin">Ahmed Yassin</a>, leader of <a href="/wiki/Hamas" title="Hamas">Hamas</a>, announces that his group is making an all-out effort to kidnap <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israeli</a> soldiers to use as bargaining chips for <a href="/wiki/Palestinians" title="Palestinians">Palestinians</a> in Israeli prisons, following the prisoner exchange between <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israel</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hezbollah" title="Hezbollah">Hezbollah</a> in which the remains of three Israeli soldiers and a businessman were exchanged for over 400 prisoners on January 29, 2004.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-223"><a href="#cite_note-223">[223]</a></sup></li>
<li>Self-confessed German <a href="/wiki/Cannibalism" title="Cannibalism">cannibal</a> <a href="/wiki/Armin_Meiwes" title="Armin Meiwes">Armin Meiwes</a> is sentenced to eight years and six months' imprisonment for <a href="/wiki/Manslaughter" title="Manslaughter">manslaughter</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-224"><a href="#cite_note-224">[224]</a></sup> The prosecution had sought a life sentence for murder.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/David_Bradley_(engineer)" title="David Bradley (engineer)">David Bradley</a>, creator of the famous "<a href="/wiki/Control-Alt-Delete" title="Control-Alt-Delete">Ctrl-Alt-Del</a>" keystroke combination, retires from <a href="/wiki/IBM" title="IBM">IBM</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-225"><a href="#cite_note-225">[225]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="January_31.2C_2004_.28Saturday.29">January 31, 2004 (Saturday)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/January_2004&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: January 31, 2004 (Saturday)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>The United States defense budget is set to exceed US$400 billion next year—an almost 7% increase—according to budget proposals inadvertently posted on <a href="/wiki/The_Pentagon" title="The Pentagon">the Pentagon</a>'s website.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-226"><a href="#cite_note-226">[226]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-227"><a href="#cite_note-227">[227]</a></sup></li>
<li>The People's Republic of China puts <a href="/wiki/Poultry" title="Poultry">poultry</a> export bans on three more areas after a <a href="/wiki/World_Health_Organization" title="World Health Organization">World Health Organization</a> warning that the chance of controlling the <a href="/wiki/Avian_influenza" title="Avian influenza">Avian flu</a> outbreak is slipping.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-228"><a href="#cite_note-228">[228]</a></sup> A new <a href="/wiki/Severe_acute_respiratory_syndrome" title="Severe acute respiratory syndrome">SARS</a> case is confirmed in <a href="/wiki/Guangdong" title="Guangdong">Guangdong</a> province.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-229"><a href="#cite_note-229">[229]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/British_Airways" title="British Airways">British Airways</a> and <a href="/wiki/Air_France" title="Air France">Air France</a> cancel five upcoming US flights to <a href="/wiki/Washington,_D.C." title="Washington, D.C.">Washington, D.C.</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Miami,_Florida" title="Miami, Florida">Miami, Florida</a> amid fears of targeting by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Al-Qaida" title="Al-Qaida">Al-Qaida</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-230"><a href="#cite_note-230">[230]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-231"><a href="#cite_note-231">[231]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-232"><a href="#cite_note-232">[232]</a></sup></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Svalbard" title="Svalbard">Svalbard</a> Undersea Cable System is officially put into operation, giving the island group at 78° North a 40<a href="/wiki/Gigabit" title="Gigabit">Gb</a> connection to the Norwegian mainland. The dual 1,440 km <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Fiber_optic" title="Fiber optic">fiber optic</a> lines from Svalbard to <a href="/wiki/Harstad" title="Harstad">Harstad</a> is needed for communicating with <a href="/wiki/Polar_orbit" title="Polar orbit">polar orbiting</a> satellite stations on Svalbard, some owned by <a href="/wiki/NASA" title="NASA">NASA</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/NOAA" title="NOAA">NOAA</a>.,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-233"><a href="#cite_note-233">[233]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-234"><a href="#cite_note-234">[234]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Copper" title="Copper">Copper</a> prices rise to a 6-year high in New York as 441 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Labor_union" title="Labor union">unionised</a> workers <a href="/wiki/Strike_action" title="Strike action">strike</a> at <a href="/wiki/BHP_Billiton" title="BHP Billiton">BHP Billiton</a>'s Cerro Colorado mine in northern <a href="/wiki/Chile" title="Chile">Chile</a> after pay negotiations fail.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-235"><a href="#cite_note-235">[235]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
